Then lance the abscess so that the excess fluid drains, and after lancing it scrape away the pus from the skin and leave only what is attached; then apply a damp cloth soaked in wine and oil, and treat with poultices and ointments until it heals.
des apostemes des ners	of the abscesses of the nerves
Ausi com aposteme vienent en l’artere et en la voine, vienent aposteme as ners quant il sont ferut, ou par trop grant travail, et semblans choses.	Also, as an abscess comes in the artery and vein, so does an abscess come to the nerves when they are bruised or from too much exertion, and similar things.
Et ceu avient plus sovent as adjutoires et as dois et en toz leus ou il ait jointures, et c’est I grief apostemes, et sa color semble la color dou cors, et est em plusors dispositions sens dolor; et quant on l’estraint forment, si sent li malaides dolor, et n’est mie em parfont dou cors, mais desoz lou keur; et muet bien de toutes pars, et ne va ne avant ne arrier, ne desoz ne desus, et celui qui est en jointures ne covient mie coper par fer: par aventure i vanroit contraction; et cil qui est ou chief ou ou front, fent le cuir au spatumile.	And this happens most often in the shoulders and elbows and throughout all joints where there are apoplexies, and it is a painful swelling, and its color resembles the color of the body, and it is in various dispositions without pain; and when one applies pressure to it properly, the patient feels pain, and it is not deep within the body but beneath the skin; and it is mute in all places, and it neither goes forward nor backward, nor downward nor upward, and that which is in joints should not be covered by iron: for perhaps there would be contraction; and that which is on the head or forehead, treat with a poultice.
Se li apostemes est petis, si le tien a unes tenailles, et le cope en sa racine; et s’il est grans, si le sospent a l’oncine, et l’escorche, puis l’oste et assemble la plaie a la costure, et lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	If the swelling is small, hold it with tweezers and cut it at its root; and if it is large, pierce it with an awl, then scrape it, then cut out the bone and close the wound with sutures, and heal it.
des grosses boces pendans	large boils hanging
Aucune fois avient en ventres et ne mie autre part thelul, et est une maladie qui est apelee «funge» par la semblance d’aus, et est li racine subtilz, et li chiez gros; et en i a de petis et de mout grans; et je vis I home qui en avoit II ou ventre qui estoient plus semblans a funges que ai autre chose, et n’i avoit point de difference, et estoient blanc, et avoient menue racine, et estoient jai fendut, et en corroit adés moistor.	At times it occurs in bellies and not elsewhere; it is a disease called "mushroom" due to its resemblance to mushrooms, with thin roots and thick stalks. There are small and very large ones; I saw a man who had two in his belly that looked more like mushrooms than anything else, without any difference, they were white, had thin roots, and were slightly split, and moisture ran from them.
Je les copai et trovai en l’un XVIII onces pesant, et en l’autre VI З., et li ovraiges en l’incision si est que tu regardes se li malaides est moistes, et li color de l’artelul est blainche et moiste et de subtil racine; si le cope au spatumile large, et soient en ta presence li cautere au feu.	I cut them and found one weighing 18 ounces and the other 6 ounces; the treatment for this is to make an incision so that you can see the moisture, and the color of the joint is white and moist with thin roots. Then apply the fire cautery widely, and have the patient hold steady so that the eyes do not move until they grow.
Car au taillier vient maintes fois trop grans decorremens de sanc, et se li sans te vaint, si te haste donques dou cauterizer; et se tu vois le malaide espoanteit et paourous de l’incision dou fer, si prent I fil de plonc bien fait, et en lie l’artelul si com nos avons dit, et le laisse II jors; et puis le restraint, et ne cesser d’estraindre lou fil de plonc tant qu’il cope l’artelul, et chiece par lui sens travail; et se les racines sont grosses, si a paour au coper meismement por le ventre, mais tu em pues bien coper la moitiet, puis le cauterize qu’il ne reviegne; puis cure la plaie, et garde que tu ne coper le thelul qui est de fuxe color et de povre sens et de lait regart.	For in cutting there are often large bleeding wounds, and if the blood stops, then quickly cauterize it; and if you see the patient is frightened and fearful of the iron incision, take a well-prepared piece of black thread, and tie the joint as we have said, and leave it for 2 days; then constrict it, and do not stop constricting the black thread until he cuts the joint, and let him heal without difficulty. And if the roots are large, it is frightening to cut into the belly, but you can certainly cut half of it, then cauterize it so that it does not return; then treat the wound, and be careful not to cut into the skin which is discolored and poor-looking and milky in appearance.Li home qui ont a funge le thelul si comme nos avons dit, covient que tu coper les arteluls et li gros estomach, et les chiez de l’estomach, et ne cesser de coper tant qu’il cope l’artelul et li chiez, et li gros estomach, et li funge.
Car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, et je venrai a la cure de chancre ci aprés.	For it is an encrusted abscess, and I will come to the treatment of cancer next.
quant li boude ist fuer	when the boil bursts
Se li apparance de la boude vient par cautere de plaie ou de fendure de syfac, et est sus le ventre et en ist aucuns des bouez, si com il avient en autres routures, ou de sanc qui cort de voines ou d’arteres selonc ceu qui est devant, ou de ventositeit; et se c’est par la routure dou syfac et par l’issue dou bouel, si est li color de l’aposteme semblans a la color dou cors, et est legiere chose sens dolor, et apert de diverse issue.	If the appearance of the boil comes from cautery of a wound or from a fissure in the syphiloma, and it is on the belly and in some of the bowels, as happens in other ulcers, or from blood which flows from veins or arteries according to what is before, or from wind; and if it is from the ulceration of the syphiloma and from the outlet of the bowel, then the color of the abscess is similar to the color of the body, and it is a light thing without pain, and it discharges in various ways.
Et se c’est por l’issue de l’intestine, adonques est il plus divers, et quant on le presse a ses dois si se repont, et puis revient, et par aventure si est sarrez, et agrandist mout a l’entree dou bain et por fort travail.	And if it is through the outlet of the intestine, then it is more diverse, and when one presses it with their fingers, it will pop back out, and sometimes it will be dry, and it will grow larger at the entrance of the bath and with great effort.
Et se c’est por moistor, c’est legiere chose, et apert bien quant tu le presses a ta main, ne ne constraint mie; et se c’est por sanc, si apert par ces signes li apostemes gros et dur, et est fichiez selonc une quantiteit; et se c’est por ventositeit, si est souef au tochier, et li ovraiges si est que tu regarde se li apparance est por le sanc de l’artere, ou de la voine, ou ventositeit.	And if it is from moisture, it is a light thing, and it opens well when you press it with your hand, and it does not constrict; and if it is from blood, then the abscesses are large and hard, and they are fixed according to a quantity; and if it is from wind, then it is soft to the touch, and the action is that you should look to see whether the appearance is due to blood from an artery or vein, or wind.
Si covient que tu laisses la cure.	If you need to let the wound heal.
Car il en a doutance et paor, si com je t’ai dit ou chapistre des apostemes, por l’artere et por la voine.	For there is doubt and fear, as I told you in the chapter on abscesses, regarding the artery and the vein.
Et se li apparance est por l’intestine ou lou boueil, si covient que tu comandes au malaide qu’il teigne son alaine, et soit estendus tout drois, puis seigne d’enche tout entor la boude; puis le comande a gesir sovin entre tes mains, puis va entor le leu que tu as signiet a tout le spatumile, puis estent la moitiet de l’aposteme au desus a tout le grant uncine; puis le lie entor d’un fil fort, ou d’une corde de fort soie fermement, et soit li nous dou liien assolz; puis oevre la moitiet de l’aposteme estendut sus le liien, et i boute ton doit indice, et quier l’intestine; se tu le trueves pris dou liien, si le deslie, et boute l’intestine au defuer dou ventre; et se tu trueves le boueil, si le prent a l’oncine, et en cope la superfluiteit; et se li artere te fait contraire, ou li voine, si vai belement entor, puis revien a ton ovraige et pren II aguilles, et i boute II fors filz, et boute les II aguilles entor ceu que tu as fait en crois que tu feis percier; puis estrain l’aposteme en IIII leus sus les aguilles, et se tu vues, oste les aguilles, et laisse lou leu tant qu’il porrisse, et chiece li char morte par soi; ou tu la cope quant elle iert subtiliie et porrie, puis le cure de ceu qu’il covient, et cheve l’aposteme si com nos avons dit; et estrai le sanc ou la moistor que tu trueves, puis cure le leu de ceu qu’il couvient, et soude le leu.	And if the appearance is in the intestines or bowels, then you should tell the patient to hold his breath and be stretched out straight, then sign all around the wound; then have him lie down between your hands, then go around the area that you have marked for the spatumile, then press down on half of the abscess above the large nail; then tie it tightly with a strong thread or strong silk rope, and let the patient's hand hang free; then work on the other half of the abscess stretched out over the rope, and insert your finger, and feel for the intestines; if you find them caught in the rope, release them from the abdomen; and if you find the bowels, grasp them at the nail and cut away the excess; and if the artery or vein is causing resistance, go around it gently and then return to your work and take two needles and thread two strong fibers through them, and insert the needles into what you have made into a cross so that you pierce it; then pull out the abscess in four places on the needles, and when you see it, remove the needles and leave the wound open until it drains, and scrape away the dead flesh by itself; when it is thin and draining, clean the wound as appropriate, and close the wound.
dou chancre	from cancer
Nos avons dit en la division les semblances de chancre, et coment on i doit ovrer par medicines, et coment on doit eschuer la cure de fer; et disons le chancre enjanreit en la marris, et grant cautele a en la cure, et dirent li ancien que quant chancres est en leu ou on le puet raier si com chancre qui est em mameles, et en la cuixe, et en semblans leus, et le doit tout oster quant il est en l’encomencement; et quant il est grans et anciens, si ne covient mie que tu l’aproches, car je n’en poi onques nul saner; ne nulz n’en sana onques devant moi.	We have already discussed the types of cancer, how to treat them with medication, and how to avoid using iron in the treatment. Now, let's talk about cancer that appears on the skin, which requires great caution during treatment. According to the ancients, when cancer is found in places where it can be easily scraped off, such as on breasts, thighs, or similar areas, it should be completely removed during its early stages. However, once it becomes large and established, you shouldn't attempt to treat it, as I have never seen anyone heal from it, nor has anyone healed from it before me.
Et li ovraiges, quant il est en leu ou on le puet oster, si com nos avons dit, est que tu purge aucune fois le malaide de cole noire; puis le fai sainier s’il ait manifeste repletion, puis afaite le malaide .i. boin leu por faire l’ovraige; puis giete tes oncines ou chancre, et le cheve de toutes pars, et l’oste de toutes pars sens rien laissier; et laisse corre le sanc tout fuer, et espreint bien le leu a ta main ou a aucune chose, et se li decorremens de sanc te fait contraire de l’incision de l’artere ou de la voine, si le cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez; puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when it is in a place where it can be removed, as we have said, you should first purge the patient with black bile; then let them bleed if there is an evident repletion; then clean the area where the cancer is located; cut off all hair, skin, and bone from the affected area without leaving anything behind; let the blood flow freely, and squeeze out any remaining blood with your hand or a tool; if the bleeding from the artery or vein opposes your incision, cauterize it until the blood vessels are sealed. Then treat the wound further until it heals.
de ydropisie	of dropsy
Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer: si est eclites soulement; et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces II semblances: c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose; donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses; si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance; et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer: lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme:	We have already discussed in the section on idiopathic edema how the accumulation of fluid occurs and the signs of each type, as well as the treatment with medication and that which is treated with iron. Only these two conditions are mentioned; one should not use iron for these two conditions: tympany and hydrops, as they are fatal. Therefore, when treating this type of edema called "eclites" with medications, and if the treatment does not help, consider whether the patient is weak or has other illnesses besides idiopathic edema, such as diarrhea and similar conditions; in that case, do not use iron, as there is a risk involved. But if you see that the patient is strong and only has idiopathic edema, and is neither too young nor too old, then proceed as follows: lift the patient straight up, and press on their abdomen to push the fluid to the lowest part of the leg, then take the spiny spatulum according to this description:
Et soit trenchans de II pars.	And it has two parts.
a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier; puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines: si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude III dois droit desoz sus lou poignil; et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude III dois; et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu; puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor; puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme:	And it has a point, and yet it is not so sharp that it can reach the intestines when pushed in, nor can it cause bleeding; then examine whether the dropsy is towards the intestines: if so, you should make your incision straight under the armpit on the right side; and if it is due to liver disease, the incision should be on the left side; and if it is due to the womb, it should be on the right, and the patient must not lie on the incision so that the fluids do not flow to that weak spot; then cut through the skin with your instrument, and insert it, and lift your hand to the spatumile between the skin and the syphon as you would when skinning a finger or toe; then pierce the syphon so that the spatumile comes out in the desired location, and this is where the water will come out; then pull the instrument out, and insert this tool from which the fluid will drain:
Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz I petit pertus; et ou costeit d’une part, III pertus; et II d’autre part, et I d’autre; et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	It resembles a fine silver needle and is made of bronze or lightweight brass, with a small hole in the lower part. The head is shaped like a feather, and this is the shape of the incision that scribes make to the quill.
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument; vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort; mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz; puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere; puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit; fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue.	at the top is the alamenol, so that when the instrument comes to the boil, it descends immediately upon the instrument; empty out half or a third of it, for if you empty more than is appropriate in that hour, by chance the patient may die from the resolution of his spirit through the weapon, or he will faint, or he will approach death; but empty it according to the quantity of its virtue, and according to what the dispositions of the patient's virtute indicate, and his pulses; then withdraw the instrument and retain the water, which is retained now by the cork that blocks the hole in the syringe, about which I have spoken, that you pierce according to this manner; then renew the instrument the following day, if you see the patient enduring it, and draw off a small quantity of water; do this every day, and be wary of causing him any pain as long as he still has some water left.

And if you doubt the disease, and you leave it with a lot of water, with hot sand or ash, and by much sweating or bathing and in the sun, and if it turns purple from drinking; and cure it with desiccating medicines until it is healed, and cauterize over the stomach and over the liver and over the spleen after the extraction of water, as I said before.
de l’estopement de la verge	on the swelling of the penis
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu.	Sometimes children are born without a foreskin, or with a small foreskin, or it is not in its place.

Those who do not have an opening in their place are bloated, for some are born with an opening at the head of the penis, which prevents them from urinating unless they lift their penis upwards; and they cannot ejaculate because the matter cannot reach the urethra, and this is a serious illness.

de la circoncision	of circumcision
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies; toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	Circumcision is not a natural process like other wounds; nonetheless, when we perform this act intentionally, especially on infants, it is necessary for us to do the best and most gentle job for their well-being.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not tell of the circumcision of their children, for they did not use it in their law, and we have only what we have acquired through experience.

dou retenement de l’urine	from the retention of urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division; et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz; et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet; et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e; et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme: et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil; et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	The retention of urine is due to a stone, or congealed blood, or a tumor, or similar things that we have mentioned in the division; and if the urine is not released, and you see that it is being retained by the stone which is lodged in the neck of the bladder, then the patient should be bent over his knees; and his feet should be placed on his back, and he should stretch his abdomen from above the back, and the patient should strain as hard as he can; and thus the neck of the bladder will be forced to expel the stone upwards, which will release the urine; and if it does not come, as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you must administer extraction using an instrument called a "syringe", which has this shape: and it should be made of thin silver, like the feather of a bird; and the cane should be about a palm and a half long, and thin at the tip.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue; et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede; puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude; puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors; puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine; et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	And the way to pass urine is to take a doubled thread and tie it to the tip of a piece of wool or cotton, and put the tip of the thread into the syringe; and squeeze out the excess wool and fill the syringe up to the tip, then anoint the syringe with oil or butter and almond oil, and have the patient sit on a seat, and raise his bladder and penis with moist oil and olive oil and warm water; then gently put the syringe into the penis until it reaches the root of the penis, then bend the penis upwards towards the scrotum; then fill the syringe up to the bladder, and feel the patient's bladder emptying, and if this is not done in this order, then the person guiding where it goes is doing it wrong; then pull out the thread all the way through the wool, and the urine follows the wool, then pull it out, and let the urine flow; and repeat with the syringe until the bladder is empty and the patient is relieved.
des maladies de la vessie	diseases of the bladder
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When blistering or bleeding occurs in the bladder, or pus is accumulated there, and you see water and medicine dripping out, then do all the apparatus that is called "clepsydra", and this is how to make it.
Elle est close, et si a III pertus: II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois; et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est; et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens; si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens; si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira; et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie: si est ci:	It is closed and has three openings: two on one side and one on the other, as you can see. The location of the hairs through which the short catheter is inserted should be such that it blocks the urethra without any additions, so that the moisture can be drawn out and injected when necessary; and when you see your medicines moving in the bladder, place the tip of the catheter into the moisture and withdraw while pulling on the other end; you will draw the moisture into the catheter and then push hard on the end that is outside. The moisture will then enter the bladder and the patient will feel it; this is the way to perform a subtle enema to cleanse the bladder: it works like this:
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut; et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet; puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu; puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie; et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor; puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument; et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	And it is made of silver or brass, and the head is higher; and under it there is a testicle or two testicles hanging; then take a sheep's bladder and put the moisture in which you want to cleanse the bladder, then tie it between the two testicles with a strong double thread, and heat this moisture over the fire; then insert the tip of the enema into the urethra, and squeeze your hand over the bladder gently until the moisture enters the bladder, and the patient will feel that the moisture has arrived in the bladder. If you do not have a bladder, take a piece of parchment, punch a hole through it, and then thread a strong wire through these holes; assemble the circle as one would assemble a quiver, and put inside what you want: oil, moisture, and water, and insert it into the instrument; and do as you did with the bladder, squeezing with your hand until the moisture reaches the bladder.
de la piere	of stone
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines; et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille; et en la vessie, et en la verge; et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	We have already discussed in the division of stones, and their extraction together with medicines; and I have said the difference between a stone lodged in the ureter, and all the signs, and in which type of stone one must operate with cutting; and in the bladder, and in the penis; and I will tell you openly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit; et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist; et a mout de ces saut li fondemens; et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont .iiij. ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece; et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	I say that the stone which is lodged in the bladder happens most often to children, and it is a sign that the urine flows from the bladder resembling water in its subtlety; and it appears yellow, and the patient feels pain in his penis, and he can urinate many times, and then it blocks up; and most of these have the foundations; and the healing is easier for children until they are 4 years old, and it is much more serious in the elderly, and it is intermediate in those who are between youth and old age; and the cure is easier for those who have large stones than for those with small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to the treatment, it is first necessary to cleanse the patient through an enema, in order to draw out all the feces that are in the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	For it sometimes blocks the search for the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut; puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval; puis la quier et la touche dedens; se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	Then take the patient by the feet and lift him up and move him about, so that the stone descends to the bottom of the bladder, and sometimes comes out from above; then let him sit between your hands, which are prepared for this purpose, and his hands should be beneath his thighs, so that the bladder is completely inclined downward; then probe and touch inside; if you feel the stone in the space, then hasten to cut on the stone.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis; et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie; puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	And if it does not come out on touching all around, then moisten your left index finger with oil, if the patient is elderly, or your middle finger, if the patient is young and strong; then insert it into his anus, and probe for the stone, and when you feel it at your finger, push it toward the neck of the bladder; then press with your finger, and push the stone out where you intend to cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille; puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	And instruct the assistant to press on the bladder with his hand, and instruct the patient to lift his testicles up with his right hand, and with his left hand pull back the skin underneath the testicles in the area where the incision is made; then insert the spatulum, which has a curved shape:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre; et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans; par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail; et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges: si est griés a issir; et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	And they make it between what is between the testicles and the anus, not in the middle but on the left side of the navel; and let it be straight on the stone, and both hands must be on the anus, and the incision must be through the belly so that it is wide by force, and narrow inside, according to the quantity of the stone, not too large; perhaps the pressure makes the testicle which is in the anus jump out without effort; and know that there is a kind of stone with angles and edges: this is difficult to extract. And there is a kind that is below, similar to a grape, and round, whose extraction is easy.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant; et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe; ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief; et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole; et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	And for those therefore that have angles and edges, make the incision larger; and if it does not jump out, you must pull with tweezers which are like a file at the end, to pull out the stone so that it does not slip; or you insert under it a small instrument curved at the end; and if you cannot grasp it thus, then widen the opening, and if the blood comes out, pull it with vitriole; and if there is more than one stone, then insert first the largest into the neck of the bladder, then push upwards, then pull out the larger ones, and the smaller ones afterwards if there are several.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	And if it is very large, then it must be cut, and a larger wound made.
Car II choses avienent au malaide: ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder; mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces; et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut; puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	For two things happen to the patient: either he dies, or the urine flows out through the opening where the wound cannot heal; but nevertheless, keep pulling it with tweezers until you have pulled it in pieces; and when you have finished your work, apply incense, aloe, and dragon's blood to the wound, then press upon it, and place a damp cloth soaked in oil and wine, or oil and rosewater and cold water, over the abscess to soothe the hot inflammation; then resew the wound on his neck, and do not loosen the bandage for three days.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you loosen it, wash the area well with oil and water, then treat the wound with thin ointment and thick ointment until it heals.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine: boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit; puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez; et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	And if hot abscesses and corrosions of blood in the bladder occur, and urine is retained because of it, in such a way that it passes out with the urine: then thrust your finger into the wound and draw out the blood, for if any remains, the bladder will be damaged and ruptured; then wash the wound with water and vinegar and celery, and treat him in every way you know how until he is healed; and it is necessary that on every day you treat him, to tie his two thighs together, and assemble the remedies over the wound.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir; si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	And if the stone is small, and it is in the passage of the penis, and stuck in, and the urine cannot come out; then the treatment of what I say below, that you cut it many times, is an excuse for cutting through this treatment.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I have tried this myself.
Pren .i. foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a .iij. angles fichiees en .i. tison:	Take a piece of iron according to this form and let it be filed into three angles:
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie; puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere; et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part; si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	Then take a thread and tie it around the penis under the stone so that it cannot return to the bladder; then push the awl into the penis gently until it reaches the stone; then turn the awl in your hand inside the stone little by little, until you pierce the stone from another side; then urine will come out immediately, after which press your hand on what is left of the stone that is inside the penis.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides; et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	If it is broken immediately and comes out with the urine and the patient is healed; but if you cannot do this for any reason that prevents it, then tie a thread under the stone and another one above it, then make an incision in the penis where the stone is between the two threads, then pull it out, and untie the thread, and clean the congealed blood in the wound; and treat it until it heals.
de la piere des femmes	of women's stones
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por .iij. choses: l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge; et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	It sometimes happens that a stone becomes lodged in women, and if it does, the cure is difficult, and is forbidden for three reasons: one is that perhaps the woman is a virgin; the second is that one cannot find a skilled woman who will submit to examination, especially if she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains; et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil; et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere; et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge: adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere; et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	And the third way is that by chance one cannot find a woman who is well skilled in this art of medicine; and the fourth way is that the stone of the woman is more deeply embedded than that of a man, so it needs to be cut deeper, and there is great fear associated with it. And if necessity arises, one should take a very knowledgeable midwife, and with difficulty persuade her, and if one cannot persuade her, then one must use a very subtle kind of mirror; and show a wise midwife the life of women, or a woman who knows part of the art, and command her to do what you command from the inquiry into the stone; and look very carefully to see if the woman is a virgin. Then she should press her finger into the urethra and search for the stone; and if she finds it, she should hold it under her finger, and recommend that she press her finger or the affected area, and squeeze and press her left hand on the bladder firmly.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse; puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie; et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite; puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont: c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	If you find it, then you should move it from the bladder entrance to below, until it reaches the root of the thigh; then press on the stone at the root of the thigh towards the middle where the testicles are, feeling for the stone in that area; do not move your finger above or below the stone, and make the incision small at first; then open the wound if you feel the stone has been cut so that it can come out, and know that there are many types of stones: some are small and large, rough and smooth, long and round, and some have veins.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	[You should] know their appearances in order to identify the exit.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez; puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre; et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide; puis cure la plaie.	And if the blood flows, then apply ground vitriol and hold it there for an hour until the bleeding stops; then return to your task, so that the stone may come out, and have the tools I mentioned for extracting the stone ready at hand to aid you in your work; and if the blood flows and it is from an artery that has been cut, then apply the powder to the wound and use bandages and binding, and do not re-open the wound, and leave the stone and do not extract it, lest the patient die; then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood has subsided and the place has healed, return to your work until the stone is out.
de hernie carnouse	of fleshy hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef; et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit .i. autre oef; et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit; et ceu n’avient se poc non.	Rupture of the waters is nothing else but an assembly of moisture or white phlegm, which is under the heart of the eggs, and is called "phlegm", and sometimes it is properly in the membrane of the egg, so that one believes it to be another egg; and it is the skin of the egg between the white phlegm that we have mentioned; and this does not happen often.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the generation of this humor is from weakness that comes to the testicles, and this matter is spread.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors: ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus; et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	And sometimes it comes from a blow to the testicles, and this moisture has many colors; it is a yellow tinge, or red-free, or black, or watery white, and so on; and these are the signs by which one can recognize this assembly, for if it is in the white syphilis that we have mentioned, there are abscesses, a little long like the shape of an egg, and it does not open the testicles, because there is moisture all around.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef; et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien; donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	And if there is moisture in the skin itself, then the abscesses are open with part of an egg, and therefore one thinks it is another egg; and if the moisture is between the skin of the testicles and the white syphilis, it feels good. Therefore, when you want to know the color of the moisture, test throughout the entire area, for its shape is as described above.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	According to this, then, what comes after the introduction, judge what is within.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors; puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz; puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions; puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir; puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont; et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement; cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue; et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac; puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when we treat it with iron, the patient should be bled according to his strength and the fullness of his body; then he should lie on his back on something slightly raised, and have lots of cushions placed under him; then he should sit up on his left side and instruct the assistant to sit on his right, and extend the rod to one of the two ribs of the heart; then take the spatulum, and cut the skin of the ribs in between them from the top down to the nipple, and make the slit straight while dissecting the skin of the ribs up to the white flesh, and scrape gently according to his strength; then pierce the sac with a large hole, and draw out all the water, and then insert your fingers, and press the sac upwards; and do not touch the heart, but only the sac; cut all around it carefully, and if you do not cut it bleeding will return; and if the egg jumps out during your work, put it back in place when you have finished working on the sac; then sew together the two edges of the skin of the ribs with a single stitch, and treat the wound as you would any other until it is healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc; puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	And if you find the testicle corrupted by some other disease, then you should ligature the vessels that are suspended, fearing the escape of blood; then cut off the testicle at its suspension, and draw it out, and dress it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices; si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset; et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	And if pus has collected into two pockets, know that they are two abscesses; then open the other part just as you did the first, equally, then wash away the blood and put in the wound soft lamb's wool moistened with rose oil; and put over the other soft lamb's wool moistened with wine and oil, and place it over the two abscesses, and place over that doubled linen and tie it up over all along its length following this form.
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil; et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier; et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers; si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	Then take two pieces of linen and stuff them with lamb's wool according to this model and sew them together along the crotch of the breeches, and one end press against the anus up to the back, and the other end at the buttock; and let the other two ends press upon the two armpits, and have all of it bound together tightly in the loop of the breeches; and sometimes this abscess is treated with cautery in place of cutting with iron, and what you do is take a very thin knife-like cautery and open up the skin over the abscesses, and when the white pus is exposed, take the cautery according to this form and pierce that abscess at its joints and scorch it with this hot cautery:
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout; et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef; et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve; et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille; et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	And cut in all ways that you can, until you reach the bone; and be careful that the fire does not touch the egg; and know that this work is safer; and be mindful of blood flow, and changes in the wound; and if nothing makes it contrary, or an abscess or blood flow or anything else, then cure what makes it contrary, according to what has been said before.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit; pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors; et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer; puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee; et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant; et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	And if the patient is fearful and does not want to undergo this treatment because of its horror, then administer perforation as I have told you, and when you are certain by the signs that we have said that the water has drained, then have the patient sit on a high seat; then pierce the abscess in the lower part all the way to the spine, and place the perforation near the spine; and make the holes large so that all the fluid flows out; then put cotton over the wound and bandage it, and leave it for the remaining fluid to drain, then treat the wound until it heals; and if the white membrane does not allow the fluid to flow out of the mouth of the wound, then you must insert a feather or the instrument used to treat the fluid in hydrophobic patients, whose form is described earlier; and widen the wound, and know that the fluid will return and be reabsorbed after six months or so, and when it has been reabsorbed as before, the patient will recover.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of the testicles
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse; et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	Know that in the treatment of this disease there are many complications, because of which I think it is better to leave it alone. And I will tell you about the treatment and the appearance of the abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions; et c’est par mout de cas.	I say therefore that many abscesses come in the body, especially in the groin; and it is by many cases.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion; et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors; et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief; et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	This is to be understood as resulting from an excess of acidity and ague, which is spread to the testicles, or from a blow; and the color of the abscess follows the color of the body; and there is no pain, and it is a serious abscess; and sometimes there are small, dark, and bloody abscesses, with a pus-like color, and occasionally they result from a burst artery, or inflammation of a vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois; et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	When it is from a burst artery, it is recognized by the hot disposition of the abscess, when you press it with your fingers; and you must not touch it.Quant li color d’aposteme est sanglant et vermeil, et par aventure est selonc la color de la fleure qu’il est venuz, ou selonc la color del corps; et est li malais grant dolor, et li membres est mal figurez: si convint que tu fasses incision sus aposteme.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars; et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	Those who are affected by inflammation of the vein are known by their appearance and the touch of the fingers; anyone can then make a diagnosis based on this, and on other symptoms. You should feel for the pulse in the scrotum, then the testicles will be drawn up, and the white sac will be protruded, and the suspensory ligament released from all parts of the testicle.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope; et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	If the testicle has become soft due to these symptoms, then you should draw it out and feel for its shape; if there is hernia in the sac, or within the vessels, then you must release all of that tendon and feel around it carefully.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the growth is in the rear location, then you must scrape all of it, and extract the egg, as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when your work is finished, then treat the wound with wool soaked in rose oil and wine, then cure it with other cures until it is healed.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of the testicles
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait; et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	This is a type of abscess wrapped in a wrapper similar to a grape, with the softening of the testicles, and the patient suffers greatly when he moves; and the cure for this disease is also very dangerous, just like the one before, and yet we will tell you about its treatment according to what the ancients did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment; puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples; puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief; puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues; puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions; car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz; si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	It is necessary that you make the patient sit on a raised seat, then tie the suspender of the testicles below your fingers, to all the vessels that are close to the penis, and stretch them properly; then cut through the spatumile at a wide angle in the center of the vessels, so that they are exposed, and then cut from each side, as we have said in the extraction of the arteries in the temples; then insert a needle where there is a double thread, and tie it to the first place where the vein appeared, and tie it directly to the other end; then pull them gently according to the length of the body, and draw out the corrupted moisture; then cure the wound as with the others by bandaging tightly, so that any vessel that supplies blood to one of the testicles is cut off; for no harm comes from this, and if blood reaches all the vessels, then the testicles should be tied at all the vessels, so that the ureter loses its nourishment due to the cutting of the vessels, and dries up and cannot function.
de la routure dou syfac	from the rot of the sinus
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions; et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes: ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses; et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement; et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	The causes of this hernia are either from the rupture occurring in the scrotum, or from the protrusion in the abdomen in the region of the groin, causing the intestines to descend from that opening towards one of the testicles; and this opening occurs either in the scrotum, or from the protrusion, and these two types of hernias arise from many causes: either from a blow, or from leaping, or from straining, or from lifting a heavy load, and from similar activities. The sign that it is from a protrusion in the scrotum is that it occurs slowly over a long period of time, and does not appear suddenly; and the hernia is even throughout, because the scrotum presses on the intestines.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the signs of sciatica are that it brings on sudden pain at the beginning, and the abscesses appear in different places under the skin, and this is for the exit of the intestines and the body to release the sciatica.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And sometimes the nerves go with the intestines, and are retained inside, and cause great pain for the patient, especially when they are pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these treatments with iron, one must avoid fear.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir; puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes; puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc; puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir; puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars; puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac; et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille; et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement; et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz; puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions; aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz; puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars; puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne; et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi; et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte; puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant; puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	And the method of treatment is that you instruct the patient to draw up the intestines inside with his hand through the opening, if he can; then have him lean forward, and hold his buttocks between your hands, and lift the scrotum upwards towards your chest; then press on the abdomen above it, and hold the skin of the testicles with your thumb and index finger, and cut around the scrotum as much as you need in order to open the hernia; then scrape away at the scrotum until the tough white membrane underneath is exposed all around; then insert your index finger into the opening behind the testicle, between the white membrane which is under the skin of the testicle and between the second membrane, and separate what is behind the testicle, and between the second membrane; and move your right hand inside the scrotum, and hold the white membrane upwards with your left hand, and lift the testicle up towards the abdomen as far as you can, and instruct an assistant to push the testicle upwards; then feel around with your fingers to see if there is any intestine wrapped around the tough white membrane, and if you find anything, pull it back into the abdomen; then take a needle with a thick thread made of 10 strands, and insert it through the back part of the scrotum, behind the testicle; then hold on to the threads with your fingers, so that there are 4 threads; then tie them together in the shape of a cross, and tightly bind the hernia with two strong knots on either side, so that none of the vessels which nourish it can enter and cause inflammation; then put the thread back into the abdomen according to the first long thread, and after these two knots leave an opening in the scrotum behind the testicle as large as a finger; and after all this, cut around the part underneath the skin of the testicles, so that the blood flows, as we have said before; then apply moistened wool to the wound, and tie up the hernia with the thread which we mentioned.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And sometimes the white syphilis that we have mentioned is cauterized after the incision, out of fear of blood flow.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui; et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece; puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	For this often happens, and let the wound bleed until it is clean; and if it is slow to bleed, use warm water, and apply what we have said, until it bleeds; then heal the wound with another remedy, until it is perfectly healed.
de hernie carnouse	of fleshy hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this remedy, I have never seen anyone dare to use fire to perform the cure.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz; puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient; et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And the ancients say that it is made like the thread which is joined to the vis, in such a way that you tie the vessels, after cutting above slightly towards the bottom; then compress with a bandage, and heal the abscess with what works, until the vessels close; and heal it as we have said, until it is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus; et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres; et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent; et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert; et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit; et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere: et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois; et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac; et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre; puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines; puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	Sometimes the rut comes out with the veins, as we have said, and opens the place; and no intestines come out into the bowels, and if any do come out, it is a little, and it repairs all hours; and even if it remains too long in this condition, the wound swells, so that the syphilis which is in the veins extends, as we have said, for it is stretched, then becomes soft and swollen and open; and its cure is by cautery, as we have said before; and sometimes it is cured by iron in this way: and let the patient lie on his back between your hands, then compress the area of the rut swollen with salt according to the quantity of three ounces; then extract the syphilis which is under the skin that sweats, then take the thread and place it over the visible area of the syphilis; and press it towards the depth of the abdomen, then tie the two visible areas of the syphilis on the thread, and tie one and the other; then extract the head of the thread, and do not compress or extend the syphilis or anything else, as I have told you in the cure of the rupture of the intestines; then heal it with the remedy for wounds.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you cut the threads, clean and treat the wound until it heals.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The syphilis is constrained, and has no appearance in the rut, and the cautery is mucous in this place, and closer to salvation.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	of the softening of the skin of the scrotum
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir; et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil; puis assemble les .ij. levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a .iij. costures ou .iiij. fermement; puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	Many times the skin of the scrotum becomes soft in some men due to the testicles within becoming softened, and it is milky white in appearance. When one wishes to treat this condition, they should make the patient lie on his back, and then cut the soft skin on top of the tunica vaginalis; next, bring the two edges of the wound together and stitch them shut with 3 or 4 stitches; then lance between the stitches and dress the wound as one would any other, until it is healed.
dou chastrement	of chastity
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre; et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres: dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure; et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	You should know that castration is forbidden in our law, and for this reason I would prefer not to mention it in this book. However, knowledge of it is necessary for two reasons: the first is so that physicians can respond knowledgeably when asked about it, and know how to perform the procedure; the second is because we often need to castrate certain animals to aid us, such as bulls, rams, goats, and other beasts.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres: ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	I say then that castration is performed in two ways: either by pulling, or by cutting.Si tu veels faire atraction, prends un filz d’asne selonc la grosseur de la testor et mets le en la fente; puis tire li filz par dessus tant qu’il rompt.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant; puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	In the type of castration that we perform by pulling, we have the animal sit in warm water until the testicles are softened and hanging loosely; then you squeeze them with your hand until they come off and you no longer feel them.Por la fendure, prends un cousteau a ta main et fends li coion en deux, tant que tu romps li corat qui est dedenz; puis tire les testors quant tu vuoies.
Du chastrement de taille: covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez; et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz; et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure; puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	Of the castration of the loin: you should hold the animal steady, and squeeze the skin of its testicles in your left hand, then tie the suspensory ligament, and beat each testicle with a stick once you have beaten them well; and leave some pus and the fine pus that is under the vessels; and this method of castration is better than that done by pulling, because when pulled, something of the testicles may remain, causing the animal to desire lust; then treat the wound until it heals.
des hermofrodites	Here is the text translated into modern English:
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes: l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	Hermaphroditism occurs in two ways in males: one is that between the testicles there appears a woman-like shape, with hair, and sometimes it discharges urine.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And the other way occurs in women, having on her groin a penis and testicles.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies; en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	And the treatment of men and women is that you treat the genitals just like other wounds; in the second method, for men whose urine passes through the skin of their scrotums, there is no cure.
de la tentigene	of the testicle
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir; et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	A tentigen is an ajosted wound above the natural part, so that it is too ugly to look at; and some women have them as large as a hand, and that is the cure.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement; et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez; et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	You should dye the excess of the tentigen with your hand or a knife, and then scrape it gently; and do not go too deep, lest bleeding occur, and then treat it with another treatment until it is healed; and for another wound that occurs at the mouth of the urethra, use cow's dung, and perhaps it will come out, and it is like the appearance of a pimple, and so they call it the "cow disease.
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	If you need to treat it, as we have said before, treat the wound until it is healed.
de erratique	of the erratic pulse
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis; et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est; ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit; et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir; et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	It is erratic when the nature of the woman is not understood, or the opening is small; and it is natural by birth, or accidental due to illness that comes to it; or it is caused by a sharp instrument, or a thin or thick syringe, and it is made profound in the sea, or on land, or below; and they must understand conception and childbirth, and perhaps flowers to possess; and the knowledge of this is through the consideration of the midwife.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If the tumors are visible nearby, then you can reach them with your fingers or a stick.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi: met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes; puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens; puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	If it is from a thin syringe, and it is nearby the lips, then you can treat it thus: place your index fingers together, and let the woman lie on her back with her legs spread; then form the lips, so that the thin syringe is pierced, and cover the tumor; then take wool, moisten it in oil, and place it on the site, and let the woman rest at home every day, so that it may not close up.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the syphilis is hard and dense, then you must cut it with a spatule similar to a myrtle leaf.
